      <div id="main">
       <b>
        25 May 2018
       </b>
       Related to the recent drawing of
       <a href="estadioazul/index.html" target="_top">
        Estadio Azul
       </a>
       , here's a drawing of parts of that stadium made into a pyramid:
       <a href="piramideazul/index.html" target="_top">
        Pirámide Azul
       </a>
       .
       <br/>
       <br/>
       <b>
        21 May 2018
       </b>
       A very realistic landscape called
       <a href="abcdefghijk/index.html" target="_top">
        abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz
       </a>
       .
       <br/>
       <br/>
       <b>
        15 May 2018
       </b>
       I've drawn something like this a few times. Doodles, mainly. This idea of an upturned pyramid with jungle on top of it. Now, though, it's got a big tower from the other side of the world behind it:
       <a href="fernsehturm/index.html" target="_top">
        Fernsehturm
       </a>
       <br/>
       <br/>
       <b>
        30 April 2018
       </b>
       Here's a drawing of
       <a href="estadioazul/index.html" target="_top">
        Estadio Azul
       </a>
       . My team of choice, Cruz Azul played in this stadium from 1996 until a couple of weeks ago. It is due to be demolished soon and will be replaced with a mall and hotel. Sigh.
       <br/>
       <br/>
       <b>
        6 April 2018
       </b>
       <a href="jacaranda/index.html" target="_top">
        Jacaranda
       </a>
       .
       <br/>
       <br/>
       <b>
        5 April 2018
       </b>
       <a href="lagoon/index.html" target="_top">
        Lagoon
       </a>
       .
       <br/>
       <br/>
       <b>
        2 April 2018
       </b>
       <a href="selfportrait2018/index.html" target="_top">
        Self-portrait
       </a>
       .
       <br/>
       <br/>
       <b>
        30 March 2018
       </b>
       A drawing of memories of being on a bus in Belize:
       <a href="hummingbird/index.html" target="_top">
        hummingbird
       </a>
       .
       <br/>
       <br/>
       <b>
        28 March 2018
       </b>
       Here's another thing that comes to you via my brain, a sketchbook, and Adobe Photoshop:
       <a href="pastpresentfuture/index.html" target="_top">
        past/present/future
       </a>
       .
       <br/>
       <br/>
       <b>
        12 February 2018
       </b>
       New drawing:
       <a href="weltraum500/index.html" target="_top">
        Weltraum500
       </a>
       .
       <br/>
       <br/>
       <b>
        9 February 2018
       </b>
       I began this in autumn 2016, fiddled with a bit here and there during 2017, and finally finished this week:
       <a href="ravepyramid/index.html" target="_top">
        Rave pyramid
       </a>
       .
       <br/>
       <br/>
       <b>
        25 January 2018
       </b>
       A few years ago, I did an infographic timeline of the
       <a href="thefall/index.html" target="_top">
        members of The Fall
       </a>
       . After the sad news of Mark E Smith's death yesterday, I've updated it. Finished it, I guess.
       <br/>
       <br/>
